```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
  else 0
}
```

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }

  // After the loop, i is the index of the last character that is not a ')'
  // (or -1 if all characters are ')').  
  // The substring s[..i+1] contains all characters before that point,
  // hence it has no trailing ')' characters.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;

  var x := |s| - i - 1; // number of trailing ')' characters
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

{

  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0

```dafny
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // After the loop, i < 0 or s[i] != ')'.
  // Thus the suffix s[i+1..] contains no trailing ')'.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{

    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;

```dafny
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

```dafny
// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

```dafny
// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

```dafny
// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{

    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1

    i := i - 1;
  }
```

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // At this point, i is -1 or s[i] != ')'
  // Therefore the trailing part of s is s[|s|-TrailingParens(s)..]
  // and the prefix that is not part of the trailing ')' is s[..i+1].
  // The number of characters in the prefix is |s| - (|s| - TrailingParens(s)) = TrailingParens(s).
  // Hence TrailingParens(s[..i+1]) == 0
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
  // After the loop, x == TrailingParens(s) and |s| - x == |s| - TrailingParens(s)
  // So bad == (TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s))
  assert bad == IsBad(s);
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
```
}

  assert i + 1 == 0 ==> TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  assert i + 1 > 0 ==> TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;

```dafny
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
```

ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }
  // After the loop i is the index of the first non-')' from the end
  // or -1 if all characters are ')'.
  // Therefore the trailing parentheses count equals |s| - i - 1.
  assert TrailingParens(s) == |s| - i - 1;
  // The remaining characters count is |s| - TrailingParens(s).
  bad := TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s);
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}
```

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])

    i := i - 1;
  }
  // At this point, i < 0 or s[i] != ')'.
  // TrailingParens(s[..i+1]) is 0 because the substring ends with a non-')' or is empty.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {
    i := i - 1;
  }

  // At this point i is -1 if the entire string was ')', otherwise i is the index
  // of the first non-')' character from the right.  Therefore TrailingParens(s[..i+1]) is the
  // number of trailing ')' characters in the suffix starting at i+1; but this suffix is
  // exactly the string of trailing ')' characters, so TrailingParens(s[..i+1]) == 0.
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;

  var x := |s| - i - 1; // number of trailing ')'
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```dafny
// Count the consecutive ')' characters at the end of the string.
// This is the mathematical definition of the problem's core concept:
// "the number of characters ')' at the end of the string."
ghost function TrailingParens(s: string): nat
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0
  else if s[|s| - 1] == ')' then 1 + TrailingParens(s[..|s| - 1])
  else 0
}

// A message is bad if the trailing ')' count strictly exceeds
// the number of remaining (non-trailing) characters.
ghost predicate IsBad(s: string)
{
  TrailingParens(s) > |s| - TrailingParens(s)
}

method InGameChat(s: string) returns (bad: bool)
  ensures bad == IsBad(s)
{
  var i := |s| - 1;

  while i >= 0 && s[i] == ')'
    invariant -1 <= i <= |s| - 1
    invariant TrailingParens(s) == (|s| - 1 - i) + TrailingParens(s[..i + 1])
  {

    i := i - 1;
  }
  assert TrailingParens(s[..i + 1]) == 0;
  var x := |s| - i - 1;
  bad := x > |s| - x;
}

```
